[《关于给予张展全面身体检查和紧急救治的呼吁书》联署名单完整版及关注张展时间线](https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_29.html)
------

<div>
<p><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;"><span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;"><span></span></span></p><a name='more'></a>张展关注组感谢<span lang="EN-GB">1216</span>位联署人及所有用各种方式在张展危难之际为她发声的海内外朋友，敬请大家继续关注狱中病危的张展和她家人、律师的处境。本联署活动在张展被判刑四年一周年（<span lang="EN-GB">2021.12.28</span>）已结束，但自由张展联署一直开放：<a href="https://www.change.org/p/china-free-citizen-journalist-zhang-zhan-%E7%AB%8B%E5%8D%B3%E6%97%A0%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E9%87%8A%E6%94%BE%E5%85%AC%E6%B0%91%E8%AE%B0%E8%80%85%E5%BC%A0%E5%B1%95"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.change.org/p/china-free-citizen-journalist-zhang-zhan-%E7%AB%8B%E5%8D%B3%E6%97%A0%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E9%87%8A%E6%94%BE%E5%85%AC%E6%B0%91%E8%AE%B0%E8%80%85%E5%BC%A0%E5%B1%95</span></a><p></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">“如果一个社会完全沉默，那么一旦有一点人类的声音，这个声音就是有关自由的抗争。”（张展）<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">《关于给予张展全面身体检查和紧急救治的呼吁书》</span></b><b><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">上海市司法局局长、上海市女子监狱监狱长：</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">我们作为公民，作为张展的朋友，作为钦佩张展良知的人，一直在关注张展的身体状况，最近从网上看到张展的哥哥所写的保外就医申请书，得知张展身体已经命悬一线，我们非常忧虑。为防止悲剧的发生，我们认为有必要写一封信给您，表达我们共同的诉求：那就是对张展进行全面的身体检查，同时对其进行紧急救治。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张展一直绝食，这不是我们这些关心张展的人愿意看到的局面，我们也曾通过不同渠道劝说张展停止绝食保重自己来日方长，但张展有自己的信仰和坚持，从辩护律师和家人会见后透露的信息，结合张展的性格看，在判决前张展绝食并非为了获得轻判的结果，判决后张展也不是为了获得保外就医或监外执行的结果。张展更为纯粹，她就是通过绝食单纯地表达对迫害的不服。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">假如张展真的有罪，哪怕她自己认为无罪而绝食，形销骨立生命垂危，从安定法秩序的角度，我们也不会附议对她保外就医或监外执行，也不会呼吁您给她全面身体检查和紧急救助。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">但是，张展是无罪的。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张展是一个逆行者，在很多人惶恐的逃离武汉时，她却只身去了武汉，这种勇气殊为难得，如果是在民族危亡时，像张展这样的人才能毁家纾难取义成仁，可以说张展这种人是一个民族最可宝贵的精神财富。张展在武汉时，大多数时间她只是静静地记录，记录武汉市民疫情下的生活，偶尔会帮助发一点求救信息，丝毫没有干扰政府的防疫救灾工作。她在疫情期间扮演的角色本质上就是一个公民记者，这样的行为怎么就寻衅滋事了？<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">在大灾大难面前，哪怕政府的力量再强大，也需要公民做一些辅助性的工作，公民逆行去灾难现场，是一个现代政府应当鼓励的行为，不仅客观上有助于救灾，而且也在塑造一种互助友爱的社会氛围，后者可能更为宝贵。对张展这种完全无害只有助益的行为动用刑事手段进行惩罚，是不义的。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">我们说张展的无罪，不仅是自然法意义上的无罪，也是实在法意义上的无罪。张展无害的行为根本没有社会危害性，也完全不符合寻衅滋事罪的犯罪构成。张展对迫害的不服从在法理情三方面都能站得住脚。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张展作为一个虔诚的基督徒，她很谦卑的看待自己，在武汉期间的行为低调谦和不事张扬，将自己隐身于其中，没有什么世俗功利的想法。如果不是上海这样一个国际大都市的公检法对她抓捕、迫害，没有多少人知道她。这是个事实，说出这点无损于张展的形象，张展就像一颗埋在海沙里的珍珠，别人是否发现她识得她，她都仍然是一颗珍珠，她自己也毫不在意。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张展现在获得的国际国内的广泛关注都是拜上海有司滥权枉法所赐，今天张展身体命悬一线，如果真的发生了死亡的悲剧，这必将会有一场国际国内谴责控诉的狂飙，那时没有谁是赢家。张展的父母失去女儿，我们失去朋友，中国失去一个优秀的公民，而你们上海公检法司将会背负永恒的历史罪责。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张展是一位你们从未见过的硬骨头，在她的字典里没有苟且这两个字，为了抗议对自己的迫害甚至不惜决志殉道，这是一个你们需要直面的现实，不要再拖延试图令她屈服，那只会进一步摧垮她的身体。我们迫切请求你们尽速给张展做全面的身体检查并给予紧急的救治，以免贻误救治的时机。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">我们之所以要求在保外就医或者监外执行之前，给张展做一个全面的身体检查并给予紧急救治，是因为我们不仅认为她应当被释放，更应当健康的活下来，而不是像一些良心犯那样在弥留之际才获准保外就医，几天后死亡而让迫害者逃脱历史的罪责。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">我们的要求并不过分，因为张展本来就是无罪的，因为张展被抓捕前是健康的，而贵局负有保障被羁押者身体不至于垮掉的职责。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Arial Unicode MS&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">公元二〇二一年十一月十二日</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">联署名单完整版（<span lang="EN-GB">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-GB">12</span>月<span lang="EN-GB">29</span>日<span lang="EN-GB">00:00 GMT</span>更新，共<span lang="EN-GB">1216</span>人，不再接受签名）</span></b><b><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">唐吉田，人权律师</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谢　阳，人权律师</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王　宇，人权律师</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">王全璋，人权律师</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李大伟，人权律师</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">6: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">马连顺，人权律师</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘书庆，人权律师</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8: </span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">22</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展在油管发布视频：“武汉后湖派出所寻方斌，案件是机密！不许拍不许录是否心虚呢？抗议烂捕公民</span><span lang="EN-GB">,</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">破坏公民知情权，滥用司法程序，方斌应无罪释放”</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://youtu.be/bNC3d5yTE-M">https://youtu.be/bNC3d5yTE-M</a><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">17</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，自由亚洲电台报道，在武汉作为公民记者采访已两个多月的上海律师张展披露，“目前武汉很多工厂继续停工，感染和无症状感染人数仍在上升”</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">https://www.rfa.org/mandarin/yataibaodao/huanjing/ql2-04172020080631.html <o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，大纪元报道，一直以公民记者身份滞留武汉的上海维权律师张展，观察到当地民生陷入窘境。她表示，物价高，生活水平下降，“人们开始一种贫民的生活。”张展这段时间持续走访各界，发现很多人精神上也处于一种很冷漠、类似斯德哥尔摩综合症的状态。人们不敢听、不敢说，也不敢把生活中一些基本的事情敞开交流，否则就被认为是搞政治。“政治这个东西其实是一个稀松平常的事情，西方社会对政治的定义是很正常化的，是人人都可以谈的，在中共的体制下，现在甚至谈吃饭生存，谈基本的生活，都搞成是谈政治。这样真的太邪恶了！”大纪元【一线采访】律师：解封后</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">武汉人生活似贫民</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">https://www.epochtimes.com/gb/20/5/2/n12077452.htm<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">13</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展在她自己的实名油管频道发布第</span><span lang="EN-GB">122</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">个小视频，是在汉口火车站前录制的：“威权防疫后果在持续显现”</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">14</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展被上海警方在武汉警方配合下跨省抓捕。张展被上海警方从武汉汉口火车站附近的宾馆被带到上海的派出所</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">15</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展被上海浦东警方以“寻衅滋事”罪名刑拘，关押在浦东新区看守所</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">18</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，保护记者委员会（</span><span lang="EN-GB">CPJ</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">）报道张展因报道武汉疫情被抓，呼吁中国当局释放张展</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，上海律和理律师事务所的戴佩清律师会见张展后称张展“一切平安”</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">19</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展的母亲在上海家中收到张展被逮捕《通知书》，通知书写道：“经上海市浦东新区人民检察院批准，于</span><span lang="EN-GB">6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">19</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日对涉嫌寻衅滋事罪的张展执行逮捕，现羁押于浦东新区看守所”</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">24</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，南华早报报道张展被批捕。</span><span lang="EN-GB">63</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">岁的张展父亲接受采访时说：我非常担心她的身体怎么样，在里面待遇怎么样，她妈妈的心都操碎了。我们一无关系，二无钱，没有办法把她弄出来。我们一点办法都没有。他还表示，对于女儿去武汉做公民记者，他是很担心的，认为她的努力不会带来变化，这么做如同鸡蛋碰石头</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，中国人权律师团律师发布关于许志永、丁家喜、张展、余文生等人案件的声明</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">18</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展案被移送检察院审查起诉</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">30</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，河南轨道律师事务所的任全牛律师接受张展母亲的委托，但次日到浦东检察院分院递交张展案子手续要求阅卷时被拒绝</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，自由亚洲电台报道张展在看守所绝食抗议，身体衰弱，需要输液</span><span lang="EN-GB">[</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">注：后来才知道，此时张展已绝食抗议多日，她进看守所后不久就绝食，从</span><span lang="EN-GB">6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月底更是正式不间断绝食，从</span><span lang="EN-GB">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月初开始被强制灌食，并受到</span><span lang="EN-GB">24</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">小时约束带及上脚镣的酷刑达数月之久。约束带是为阻止她拔鼻饲管，脚镣则为惩罚她绝食</span><span lang="EN-GB">]<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，戴佩清律师会见张展后说张展”抗拒进食“，”并且准备一直这样下去“，已经造成营养不良、贫血、低血压，但称其“比想象中好”、”无比平安喜乐“</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">29</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，闻宇律师会见张展。张展不妥协，绝食已五个多月，仍在继续绝食。闻宇律师因受到压力无法继续代理。这是首次确认张展遭羁押后不久即已开始绝食。自由亚洲电台报道：“张展绝食逾五个月不妥协</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，李大伟律师与张展母亲通电话后在推特发布关于张展案的通报：戴佩清律师最近会见了张展，张展仍在看守所绝食抗争；戴未告知张展家属起诉书内容；办案国保曾告知家属，张展在武汉时编造的谎言（政府对武汉市民普遍进行核酸检查时收费；封城期间，小区保安给住户配送腐烂变质的蔬菜）。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">13</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，李大伟律师在推特公布张展的起诉书及量刑建议书。此后张展案引起西方媒体广泛关注报道。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">15</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，美国视觉艺术家协会（</span><span lang="EN-GB">Visual Artists Guild) </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">在巴沙迪那市举行汽车游行葬礼活动，纪念武汉病毒受害者、李文亮、全球死于武汉病毒者，要求中国释放公民记者陈秋实、方斌、张展，并允许国际研究人员前往武汉研究病毒源</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">17</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，人权组织“中国人权捍卫者”（</span><span lang="EN-GB">CHRD</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">）针对张展、端点星案的陈玫、蔡伟的案件，向联合国提出申诉案</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">11</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">21</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">日，张展起诉书中列为“证人”之一的王定邦发布声明：《我虽懦弱苟且，亦绝做不出构陷义人的恶行</span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"> </span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">——关于张展起诉书中我的所谓“证言”的声明》</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">11</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">22</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">日，张展起诉书上所列证人之一王定邦发表视频声明</span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"> </span><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://youtu.be/77pt1iN-88k"><span style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">https://youtu.be/77pt1iN-88k</span></a></span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">11</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">23</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">日，张科科律师阅卷并会见张展。之后通报说，张展“明显瘦了很多，不管是脸型还是身型。脸色发白“，”因长期绝食，遭到同监室人强迫喂食，更多时候通过插管灌食。导致胃疼，头晕目眩，走路乏力。也无力外出放风，终日未见阳光“，”血压较低”。她“认为自己没有罪，对有关证据也不认可”</span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"> </span><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2020/11/blog-post_96.html"><span style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2020/11/blog-post_96.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">自由亚洲电台报道：“公民记者张展拒绝认罪</span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"> </span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">囚室内鼻饲流质食物”</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="background: white; color: #333333; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">12</span><span style="background: white; color: #333333; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">One Free Press Coalition (</span><span style="background: white; color: #333333; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">“</span><span style="background: white; color: #333333; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">十位最紧迫</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="background: white; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="background: white; color: #333333; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">10 Most Urgent</span><span style="background: white; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">12</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">8</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">日，张科科律师再次会见张展。申请同时会见的任全牛律师被拒绝会见。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">12</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">9</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">日，张科科律师、任全牛律师递交取保候审申请书</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">12</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">9 </span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">日，张科科律师通报会见情况，说张展“头发蓬松，口罩蒙面。揭开口罩，口鼻处插着胃管。穿着较厚睡衣，腰间围一约束带，前后别着左手右手。她说近日又插了胃管，因为她想拔掉，便被上了约束带。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">24</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">小时束缚，上卫生间需要旁人辅助，睡觉只能翻来覆去”，“除了头痛头晕、胃疼，还有口腔和咽喉的疼痛，可能有炎症，因为插胃管原因”。张展说“心力交瘁，每一天都是煎熬”，从祷告、背诵经文中得到安慰</span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"> </span><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://www.chinaaid.net/2020/12/blog-post_18.html"><span style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">https://www.chinaaid.net/2020/12/blog-post_18.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">12</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">10</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">日，国际特赦组织为张展发起紧急救</span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">援活动</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">12</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">11</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">日，美国</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">CBS</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">新闻网报道张展绝食抗争遭强制灌食、被绑缚约束带的情形，张展律师说她可能无法活着出狱</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">12</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">11</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">日，日本电视台</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">NNN</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">播出张展母亲访谈</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">12</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">16</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">日，张展的辩护律师收到开庭通知：张展被控寻衅滋事案将在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">2020</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">12</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">28</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">日</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">9:30</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">于上海浦东新区法院第九法庭开庭审理</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">12</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">17</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">日，任全牛律师在上海浦东看守所首次见到张展</span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"> </span><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://www.msguancha.com/a/lanmu50/2020/1217/20543.html"><span style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">https://www.msguancha.com/a/lanmu50/2020/1217/20543.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">“在她摘下口罩的瞬间我看到了一个完全‘脱像’的张展！因为我们都是在网路上看到过她的相片，头发浓厚面部肥实，一看就不是瘦小的人，而这一面看她，完全不是同一个人了，面容苍白有皱褶，瘦的几乎就是皮包骨，因她身高大约在一米八左右，虽然冬天穿着一层厚棉衣，但仍能看出她瘦的几乎就是走路都打晃，几乎无法支撑自己高大的身体。同时也看到，她的鼻子里仍然插着那个强制灌食的塑料管儿。张展女士的心路历程简单总结便是：她作为一名笃信基督的人，在她近些年逐渐觉醒的情况下，她便无法再‘岁月静好’下去了，虽然她曾经有很好的收入不错的工作，但她觉得，作为一个人她不能无视身边发生的罪恶与不义，她无法忍受发生在自己所处社会里人们的苦难，她要在坚定对神的信仰之下做自己认为正确的事。她无法接受谎言与欺骗，更不愿意与黑暗共生，她被抓以后，仍然常常祷告，要为那些恶人罪人祷告赎罪，她绝食不是为了争取个人获自由，她觉得抓捕她就是这个社会对好人的迫害，在看守所里，她无法若无其事的该吃吃该喝喝的度过每一天，她要用绝食来表达自己最强烈的不配合罪恶迫害的态度！她甚至表达了只要一天没有迎来她期望的大光明，一天还在被迫害的环境中，她就不会停止绝食。虽然，我也试图用她能理解的方式劝慰她要保重，要明白自己到底在做什么，她都是坚定的回答她很清楚自己的所为。”</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">21</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展关注组成员丁建强（网名河山硕）在洛杉矶因感染武汉肺炎病毒不幸去世</span> <span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">12</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">21</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">日，保护人权捍卫者观察站（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">The Observatory for the Protection of Human Rights Defenders</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">）为张展发起紧急救援行</span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">动</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">25</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日下午，张科科律师在上海浦东新区看守所见到张展</span> <span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2020/12/3_26.html"><span style="background: white; color: #1155cc;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2020/12/3_26.html</span></a><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">26</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展关注组发布三张张展在浦东新区看守所中的照片</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="background: white; color: #333333;">12</span><span style="background: white; color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="background: white; color: #333333;">27</span><span style="background: white; color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，马修凯、周静安、李汉桥等武汉市民为张展呼吁——敬请关注公民记者张展</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="background: white; color: #333333;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://mobile.twitter.com/changchengwai/status/1343161935831982081"><span style="background: white;">https://mobile.twitter.com/changchengwai/status/1343161935831982081</span></a><span style="background: white; color: #333333;"> <o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="background: white; color: #333333;">12</span><span style="background: white; color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="background: white; color: #333333;">27</span><span style="background: white; color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日夜，张展案开庭前几个小时，曾公开声援张展的彭永和律师一度失</span><span style="background: white; color: #333333; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">联</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展在上海浦东新区法院受审，被当庭宣判以寻衅滋事罪判处四年监禁。张展的母亲在法庭聆听宣判结果后，在法院外放声大哭。她接受</span><span lang="EN-GB">RFA</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">采访时说，作为母亲，看到绝食多月的女儿骨瘦如柴，悲痛万分，她更痛斥“当局惨无人道”。她说，七个多月来，她配合国保，谢绝所有外媒采访，但是法官仍然重判她的女儿，张母向自由亚洲电台说：“他们这是想置张展于死地…我以前没有配合律师，我是配合了警察。我觉得我上当了。没想到判得太重了。”</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">张科科律师：“当法院判决结果下来时，张展好像有点震惊，因为她没想到法院真的会判的这么重。”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">任全牛律师说，张展今天看起来仍然很虚弱，在被宣判后“她显得非常难过”，“感到很震惊，没想到会这么重“，任律师表示对张展的精神状态感到“非常担心”。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">张展开庭日，九位到法院附近的支持者一度被警方带走，扣押在世纪广场派出所。陕西天水李大伟律师后被当地国保约谈。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">张展在法庭上的发言：</span><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/1k79ZIKNVZdJ17yWTy-dJ_Lu0u8UaSoVt/">https://docs.google.com/document/d/1k79ZIKNVZdJ17yWTy-dJ_Lu0u8UaSoVt/</a><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">【“公检法如果要对人民审查，可以把任何人推上法庭”】——张展案庭审辩论阶段·辩护律师部分口头发言</span><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://drive.google.com/file/d/1ZCh8cr3gkPK7k6KFkfoBI98jEodBHcrY/">https://drive.google.com/file/d/1ZCh8cr3gkPK7k6KFkfoBI98jEodBHcrY/</a><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">港人</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/1dQ4QJTdbBWIpggxk5ZY5xS_WgGQmIJEabbUddso8FzA">https://docs.google.com/document/d/1dQ4QJTdbBWIpggxk5ZY5xS_WgGQmIJEabbUddso8FzA</a><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">2021</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-GB">2021</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB">1</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">1</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展被列为</span><span lang="EN-GB">One Free Press Coalition </span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">当月最危急记者关注名单榜首</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，基督徒群体发起“接力禁食祷告</span> <span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">陪张展姊妹行苦路”倡议</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/1rGgRjivJf5eBrPPzhzTJqA9DUgDjSaHv7vYDjyowk34">https://docs.google.com/document/d/1rGgRjivJf5eBrPPzhzTJqA9DUgDjSaHv7vYDjyowk34</a><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张科科律师会见张展</span> <span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://drive.google.com/file/d/118Ou_SNNNonP-m8RnWk5-QtPPqH8Pgml/">https://drive.google.com/file/d/118Ou_SNNNonP-m8RnWk5-QtPPqH8Pgml/</a></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">张展仍处于半绝食状态，至少目前没有灌食和束缚。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，国际特赦组织再次为张展发起紧急救援行动</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">13</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张科科律师最后一次会见张展。张展没有上诉，表明会坚持半绝食；绝食日久后进食会胃痛；看守所威胁用更粗的胃管对她进行强制鼻饲。张展说她不想上诉，因为“不想在封闭的逻辑圈打转”。她认为，上诉除了引起他们紧张、防卫的情绪以外，不会敲打他们的心。“只有连接耶稣基督，只有上帝的大爱才能触动他们。我认为外界的关注不能让他们悔改。”关于绝食，张展说：“只要在看守所一天，无法违背自己的内心如常吃饭。吃饭表示我承认我是一个被关押在这里的罪犯。”她讲她也对看守所的人员说：“你们的敌人不是我，恐怕是天上看不见的恶魔。”</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">她说她常常趴着看守所的栏杆“演讲”，“用最大的声音”传递她的态度。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/01/blog-post_72.html<o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展辩护律师之一任全牛律师被吊销律师证</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，腊月二十二，张展母亲用警察手机首次与看守所中的张展视频见面，连线二十几分钟，数次中断。张展坚持半绝食，身体状况堪忧。面对劝她恢复正常吃饭的母亲，她说：“对不起”。当天张展已在看守所被隔离，准备转到监狱服刑。后家属多次询问张展被转送到哪里，看守所拒绝告知。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展关注组发布张展在法庭受审照片</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><a name="more"></a><span lang="EN-GB">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，德国之声报道：张展在狱中继续绝食抗议</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">21</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展关注组：张展已被转到上海女子监狱（上海市松江区泗泾镇张泾路</span><span lang="EN-GB">1601</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">号，邮编</span><span lang="EN-GB">201601</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">），家属要求探监遭拒</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日世界新闻自由日，布鲁塞尔自由大学将</span><span lang="EN-GB">Difference Day </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">言论自由荣誉奖颁给狱中中国公民记者张展</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日德国之声报道：张展转到监狱服刑，家人仍未得到探监权及通信权</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">31</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展被送到监狱医院，绑在“死人床”上强迫灌食</span><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">天</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">（</span><span lang="EN-GB">RFA</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">报道</span><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;<a href="https://www.rfa.org/.../renquanfazhi/ec-08232021063302.html">https://www.rfa.org/.../renquanfazhi/ec-08232021063302.html</a></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">）</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">号，家人与张展通话，得知张展的身体状况很不好，于</span><span lang="EN-GB">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">31</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">号住院，体重不到</span><span lang="EN-GB">40</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">公斤，因半绝食造成营养严重不良，腿脚浮肿很严重。家人劝张展定要正常吃饭，她仍然坚称自己无罪，不会正常吃饭</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">（张展母亲微信群通报）</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">8</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">9</span><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">日，张展关注组发起</span><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"> </span><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/1QP8QXVKmB05sDdj6i6dhdF_SxBNrbDYs22-hc5WHajY/edit?usp=sharing"><span style="color: #1155cc; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;">#</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color: #1155cc; font-family: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;"><span lang="EN-US">救张展</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color: #1155cc; font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-ansi-language: EN-US;"><span lang="EN-US"> </span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color: #1155cc; font-family: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;"><span lang="EN-US">网友联署活动</span></span></a> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">（共</span><span lang="EN-GB">638</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">人参与）</span><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://docs.google.com/document/d/1QP8QXVKmB05sDdj6i6dhdF_SxBNrbDYs22-hc5WHajY/">https://docs.google.com/document/d/1QP8QXVKmB05sDdj6i6dhdF_SxBNrbDYs22-hc5WHajY/</a><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">23</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，自由亚洲电台报道：</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">公民记者张展体重急跌</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">家属要求保外就医被拒</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">。张展持续绝食抗争一年多，于</span><span lang="EN-GB">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">31</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日被送到监狱医院，绑在“死人床”上强迫灌食</span><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">天。张展坚持自己无罪，不肯停止绝食，</span><span lang="EN-GB">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日回到监狱。她体重下降一半，严重营养不良、胃溃疡、食管炎，母亲担心会器官衰竭</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">17</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，无国界记者（</span><span lang="EN-GB">RSF</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">）与其他</span><span lang="EN-GB">44</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">家非政府组织联名公开致信习近平，要求无罪释放被判刑四年、狱中绝食病危的张展</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，国际特赦为张展发起</span><span lang="EN-GB"> Write for Rights</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">活动：</span> <span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://youtu.be/YhsJ-K4cUwQ">https://youtu.be/YhsJ-K4cUwQ</a> <o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://www.amnesty.org/en/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/ASA1744262021ENGLISH.pdf">https://www.amnesty.org/en/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/ASA1744262021ENGLISH.pdf</a><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">13</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展的代理律师张科科律师向女子监狱递交申请会见的材料</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">14</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展母亲对关心张展的朋友表示，她只得到一次与女儿视频通话的机会，只有四分零九秒就结束了。她得知张展在监狱医院被绑约束带强制鼻饲</span><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">天，后来回到监狱</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">29</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展母亲在微信群发出消息：与张展视频通话中看到张展情况更危急，身体状况更加虚弱，“要人扶着走路，说话时连头都无力扬着，再不保外就医，很危险！”</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">30</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展哥哥在推特开始发系列推文，表示妹妹生命垂危。他发了张展</span><span lang="EN-GB">2007</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">年念大学时的几张照片及一张童年的照片。“张展身高</span><span lang="EN-GB">177cm</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">，目前体重不足</span><span lang="EN-GB">40kg</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">。她那么倔强。我觉得她可能活不了太久了。在即将到来的冷冬，如果她没有坚持过去，我希望世界能记住她原来的样子。”“如果张展因为记录、评论了</span><span lang="EN-GB">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">年有关武汉疫情的几件真实的事件，就被抓捕、判刑四年，行将因饥饿而死去，那么微博上这么多为云南瑞丽疫情呼救的人，也都要被抓起来吗？”“一直在劝她保重自我。她似乎不会。我母亲前天看完她回来，哭了很久，面容枯槁、满眼悲伤。因为张展看起来已经病入膏肓，身形完全走样。她心里似乎只有上帝和她认定的公理，其他全然不顾。我可怜我的父母，</span><span lang="EN-GB">65</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">岁了还要遭此劫难。”</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月底，张展再次因病危送院</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，国际特赦、无国界记者、人权观察三家国际人权机构分别发布声明，呼吁中国当局释放张展。其中人权观察还呼吁各国驻华外交官向中国当局要求探视狱中病危的张展，如遭拒，他们应该自行去监狱要求会见，以表达对张展处境的严重关切。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，谢阳律师欲赴沪探望张展母亲，以健康码突然变色被拦阻。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，魏水平律师赴沪，在张展母亲住所附近被绑架、拘留并强行送回深圳。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展哥哥张举向上海监狱管理局网站递交《请予以张展保外就医的申请》：“尊敬的各位领导：</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">我是张展的哥哥张举。张展目前被关押在上海市女子监狱第五监区，她的监号为</span><span lang="EN-GB">27997</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">。</span><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月份，我们在女子监狱的会客室，与被送至医院的张展以及医生通了电话。从中得知，张展的身体极为羸弱，体重不足</span><span lang="EN-GB">40</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">公斤。张展身高</span><span lang="EN-GB">177</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">厘米，正常体重是</span><span lang="EN-GB">60-65</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">公斤。自张展被关押至浦东看守所，到转押至女子监狱期间，因为种种原因，张展的身体羸弱不堪。我问医生，张展是否可能死去？医生明确回答我可能性很大。</span><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">29</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，我母亲得到监狱通知，去监狱和张展进行了视频会见。我母亲见到的张展，比我们在</span><span lang="EN-GB">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月份电话中听到的还要虚弱，张展的体重恐怕更加不足</span><span lang="EN-GB">40</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">公斤，走路需要人搀扶，脖子无力支撑脑袋，脸上和额头上皮包骨头、毫无血色，已经命悬一线。张展目前的身体状况不能独自走路。在搀扶和支撑下，勉强可以行走</span><span lang="EN-GB">20-30</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">米的距离。我母亲闻此噩耗，万分悲痛，甚至向监狱工作人员双膝下跪，希望他们能给予张展人道的照顾。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">长时间的关押和饥饿给张展的内脏器官和分泌系统带来不可逆转的损伤。根据《最高人民法院、最高人民检察院、公安部、司法部、国家卫生计生委关于印发《暂予监外执行规定》的通知》的相关规定，张展目前的身体条件和身患疾病，已经符合“保外就医”的相关条件。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">无论从相关法律规定或者人道主义原则出发，我们特此申请，请批准允许张展保外就医。我们深知，张展案件具有一定的敏感性。从家人的角度，我们愿意配合警察、监狱等相关部门的相关要求。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">”</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日上海市监狱管理局答复张举的申请：”答复：</span> <span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">你好！你可以致电女子监狱刑罚执行科咨询具体事宜。</span><span lang="EN-GB">021-57615998</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">转刑罚执行科。“</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日</span> <span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">美国国务院发言人普莱斯在记者会上对遭到中国当局监禁的公民记者张展的处境深表关切。他呼吁中国立即无条件释放张展，并呼吁北京尊重新闻自由和人民自由表达意见的权利。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，华盛顿邮报编辑部发表题为“她曾讲述武汉真相，现在她在中国监狱中濒临死亡”的社论</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，</span><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://cn.wsj.com/articles/%E4%B8%AD%E5%9B%BD%E5%9C%A8%E5%9B%9A%E8%AE%B0%E8%80%85%E5%BC%A0%E5%B1%95%E7%97%85%E6%83%85%E5%8D%B1%E9%87%8D-%E6%AD%A4%E5%89%8D%E5%9B%A0%E6%8A%A5%E9%81%93%E6%AD%A6%E6%B1%89%E7%96%AB%E6%83%85%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-11636523410"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ansi-language: EN-US; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;"><span lang="EN-US">华尔街日报报道</span></span></a></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">：中国在囚记者张展病情危重，此前因报道武汉疫情入狱。张展因疫情早期在武汉拍摄的视频报道而遭中国关押，据她的家人和律师称，她在狱中自发绝食后病情危重。张展的哥哥说，他认为妹妹被判处的刑期特别长，原因是她以前曾多次与当局发生过冲突，而且她这次在整个拘留和审判过程中不妥协，认为自己没有做错什么事。据张举说，</span><span lang="EN-GB">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">年，张展曾在上海一处公共场所举着要求共产党下台的标语牌，她因此在未经审判的情况下被拘留了几个月。他说，那次警方的反应让他妹妹更加坚定地批评政府，并就不公正现象发声。家人给狱中的张展写了几封信，劝她吃点东西以保持体力，但只是徒劳。张举说，张展经常回信说绝食是她反抗当局的最后手段。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">据张举说，与此同时，上海女子监狱以疫情风险为由禁止张展的家人面对面探视。张举说，由于狱方不认可他与张展的兄妹关系，他还被禁止与张展视频对话。自张展入狱以来，她的父母获准与女儿进行了三次现场视频对话，每次对话时间限制在</span><span lang="EN-GB">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">分钟左右。张举说，天气越来越冷，他担心张展能不能熬过接下来的几个月。他说，他们的母亲特别心疼，</span><span lang="EN-GB">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月份时她从监狱回来，哭着说张展脸色苍白，连站立都需要工作人员搀扶。他还说，张展与另外五名囚犯关在一间牢房里，只有几次被允许到牢房外几米远的地方活动。他说，家里人当然希望她能安全出来。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">张展的律师称，上海女子监狱一再拒绝他与他的当事人接触。他称，张展用绝食的方法抗争，反对当局对她的案件从拘捕到检控的所有处理方式。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">张展的哥哥说，张展家在陕西省，从小家境比较富裕，她大学时学习保险和金融，后来在上海做律师。</span><span lang="EN-GB">2013</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">年左右，她开始对人权和民权活动产生兴趣，当时她皈依了基督教。</span><span lang="EN-GB">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月，家人得知张展去了武汉，他们叮嘱她小心别被感染，几乎没有注意到她发布的视频报道。张举称，直到</span><span lang="EN-GB">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月警方拘捕了张展，把她带回上海，他们才得以全面了解她的新闻报道内容，以及这些行动在政府看来有多严重。张举称，他曾经和妹妹聊到让她移居到国外，他说你到美国那里可以更自由地表达自己的观点。但他说，妹妹总是拒绝此想法，并越来越坚定地与政府抗争。他回忆道，张展说“中国的问题应该在中国解决”。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展母亲在微信群中说，她致电上海女子监狱，被接线员告知要其递交书面申请</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><a name="_Hlk91625826"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk91625826;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">11</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk91625826;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展哥哥最后一次转推，自此不再更新推特。最后发于</span><span lang="EN-GB">11</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk91625826;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">9</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk91625826;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日的推文是“救救张展，允许她保外就医！”</span></span><a href="https://twitter.com/Jeffreychang81/status/1457992259064922114"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk91625826;"><span lang="EN-GB">https://twitter.com/Jeffreychang81/status/1457992259064922114</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk91625826;"></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk91625826;"><span lang="EN-GB"> <o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk91625826;"></span> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">13</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展母亲所在关注张展微信群被封</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">14</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，《关于给予张展全面身体检查和紧急救治的呼吁书》公布，联署活动开始</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">15</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展母亲到上海女子监狱递交保外就医书面申请，被告知监狱防疫政策是，材料交到门房需要等</span><span lang="EN-GB">48</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">小时消毒，之后才送狱政科。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">18</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，无国界记者宣布中国公民记者张展获</span><span lang="EN-GB">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">年新闻自由勇气奖。</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">19</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，联合国人权高专办发表声明，呼吁至少从人道出发释放张展，提供医疗救治</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">22</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，联合国八位人权专家发布联合声明，呼吁释放张展</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">23</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，欧盟发布声明，要求中国政府给予张展及时充分医疗救治，让她见家属、律师</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">24</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张科科律师受张展家属委托，到上海监狱管理局交涉律师会见受阻、家属申请保外就医无进展，无人接待</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">30</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展家人获许与张展视频通话，但未通报情况</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB" style="background: white; color: #333333;">12</span><span style="background: white; color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="background: white; color: #333333;">1</span><span style="background: white; color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展再次登上</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="background: white; color: #333333;">One Free Press Coalition </span><span style="background: white; color: #333333; font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">最危急记者关注名单榜</span><span style="background: white; color: #333333; font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">首</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，美国国会及行政当局中国委员会呼吁立即</span><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;#</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">释放张展</span><span lang="EN-GB">&nbsp;#</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">奥运囚犯</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，无国界记者组织发布报告《中国新闻业大跃退》，其中包含中国当局对武汉疫情期间独立记者的打压，个案中突出张展案</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，对华援助协会在美国华府举办林昭自由奖颁奖仪式，高智晟、张展获奖</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展母亲对南华早报记者确认保外就医申请仍无回音，但拒绝就张展情况说什么（南华早报</span><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日报道：</span><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://www.scmp.com/news/china/politics/article/3159331/jailed-chinese-citizen-journalist-zhang-zhan-explains">https://www.scmp.com/news/china/politics/article/3159331/jailed-chinese-citizen-journalist-zhang-zhan-explains</a></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">）</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，国际人权日，《关于给予张展全面身体检查和紧急救治的呼吁书》首位联署人、人权律师唐吉田失联</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">14</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，李大伟律师与张展母亲通电话。据张妈妈说，</span><span lang="EN-GB">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月底她获许与张展视频通话，张展仍然虚弱，走路仍需搀扶，情况堪忧；狱方曾在</span><span lang="EN-GB">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月底送张展到医院，但未将检查结果告知张展家人。详情不知：张展住院多久、接受何种治疗、有无被强制灌食、目前体重多少（</span><span lang="EN-GB">RFA2021.12.28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">报道：公民记者张展入狱一周年</span> <span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">拒不让步难保外就医</span><span lang="EN-GB"><a href="https://www.rfa.org/mandarin/yataibaodao/renquanfazhi/gf-12282021092703.html">https://www.rfa.org/mandarin/yataibaodao/renquanfazhi/gf-12282021092703.html</a></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">）</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">24</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，华人民主书院等台湾人权机构与台湾跨党派议员开记者会，呼吁中国当局勿以“国家安全”践踏人权与亲情，声援张展、郭飞雄、唐吉田</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">27</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，无国界记者发表声明，纪念中国记者张展被判刑一周年，呼吁释放狱中奄奄一息的张展</span><span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-GB">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB">28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Arial; mso-hansi-font-family: Arial;">日，张展被判刑一周年，《关于给予张展全面身体检查和紧急救治的呼吁书》联署活动结束，共</span><span lang="EN-GB">1216</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;
